3.2 BASIC FACTS ABOUT AFFECT RURAL FAMILIES FOUND IN THE SURVEY
3.2.1 NUMBER OF FAMILY MEMBERS
The survey of rural families involved 1,848 persons including 891 women,
accountirig for 48% of the total number of people surveyed, and 1,015 labourers,
accounting for 55% of the total number. No minority nationalities were involved in the
survey. See
TABLE 3-2 for detail.
3.2.2 AGE STRUCTURE OF THE POPULATION
Of the 1,848 people surveyed, 230 were under 6 years of age, accounting for 12% of
the total number, 411 were within 7-15 years of age, accounting for 22%, 989 were
within 16-60 years of age, accounting for 54%, and 218 were above 60 years of
age, accounting for 12% of the total number. See
TABLE 3-2 for detail.
SOGREAH CONSULTANTS - 23500321.R4 - AUGUST 2004                    PAGE 58



CHONGQING MUNICIPALITY - THE WORLD BANK
CHONGQING URBAN ENVIRONMENT PROJECT
RESETTLEMENT ACTION PLAN
3.2.3 EDUCATION BACKGROUND
Of the 1,848 people surveyed, 108 were illiterate, accounting for 5.46% of the total
number, 476 attended primary school, accounting for 26%, 917 attended secondary
school, accounting for 50%, 337 attended high school, accounting for 18%, 9
attended college, accounting for 0.49%, and 1 attended university and above,
accounting for 0.05%. See
TABLE 3-2 for detail.
3.2.4 EMPLOYMENT OF LABORERS
The 1,848 people surveyed included 1,015 labourers, of whom, 524 were working as
farmers at home, and accounting for 53% and 481 were working as migrant workers
away from home, accounting for 47%. See
TABLE 3-2 for detail.
3.2.5 ANNUAL FAMILY INCOME AND EXPENDITURE
See TABLE 3-3 for the annual income and expenditure of rural families.
3.3 BASIC FACTS ABOUT AFFECTED URBAN FAMILIES FOUNDING IN THE
SURVEY
3.3.1 NUMBER OF FAMILY MEMBERS
The survey of urban families involved 270 persons in 55 households including 117
women, accounting for 43% of the total number of people surveyed, and 145
labourers, accounting for 54% of the total number. No minority nationalities were
involved in the survey. See TABLE 3-4 for detail.
3.3.2 AGE STRUCTURE OF THE POPULATION
Of the 270 people in 55 households surveyed, 25 were under 6 years of age,
accounting for 9% of the total number, 69 were within 7-15 years of age, accounting
for 26%, 147 were within 16-60 years of age, accounting for 54%, and 218 were
above 60 years of age, accounting for 11 % of the total number. See TABLE 3-4 for
detail.
SOGREAH CONSULTANTS - 23500321 R4 - AUGUST 2004         PAGE 59



CHONGOING MUNICIPALITY - THE WORLD BANK
CHONGQING URBAN ENVIRONMENT PROJECT
RESETTLEMENT ACTION PLAN
3.3.3 EDUCATION BACKGROUND
Of the 270 people in 55 households surveyed, 1 was illiterate, accounting for 0.4% of
the total number, 95 attended primary school, accounting for 35%, 95 attended
secondary school, accounting for 35%, 63 attended high school, accounting for 23%,
1 attended college, accounting for 0.4%, and 10 attended university and above,
accounting for 4%. See TABLE 3-4 for detail.
3.3.4 EMPLOYMENT OF LABORERS
The 270 people in 55 households surveyed included 145 labourers, of whom, 71
stayed at home doing housework, accounting for 49% and 74 were employed,
accounting for 51 %. See TABLE 3-4 for detail.
3.3.5 ANNUAL FAMILY INCOME AND EXPENDITURE
See TABLE 3-5 for the annual income and expenditure of urban families.
3.4 BASIC FACTS ABOUT THE AFFECTED ENTERPRISES FOUND IN THE
SURVEY
The socio-economic survey covered the situation of the affected enterprises in
operation and the salary level of their employees. See TABLE 3-6 for detail. Of the
15 enterprises, 6 are by privates, 7 by the collective, 1 by the state and I is a stock
company. Except two enterprises that had stopped production and one that operated
seasonally, all the 13 enterprises are operating quite well and the average monthly
salary level of their employees is within RMB500-2,500.
3.5 BASIC FACTS ABOUT THE AFFECTED INSTITUTIONS FOUND IN THE SURVEY
The socio-economic survey covered the situation of the affected institutions and the
salary level of the workers. See TABLE 3-7 for detail. There are 3 institutions to be
affected by the project and the average monthly salary level of the workers there
was RMB850-1150.
3.6 BASIC FACTS ABOUT THE AFFECTED SHOPS FOUND IN THE SURVEY
The socio-economic survey covered the situation of the affected shops in operation
and the income level of the shop owners. See TABLE 3-8 for detail. Of the 38
affected shops, 36 were private shops and most of them are in the residential
houses built along the street or riverside. Most of the shops are run by the owners of
the residences themselves. The shop assistants are basically the owners' own family
members. There are only one collective-run shop and one state-owned shop.

4 LAWS AND POLICY FRAMEWORK
4.1 MAIN LAWS AND POLICIES OF RESETTLEMENT
* Law on Land Administration of the People's Republic of China (effective on January 1, 1999)
* Law on Urban Real Estate Assets Administration of the People's Republic of China (effective on
January 1, 1995)
*  Regulations on Urban Housing Dismantling and Resettlement Administration (effective on
November 1, 2001)
* Provisions on Land Administration of Chongqing Municipality (Chongqing Municipal Government
Decree No. 53, on March 30, 1999)
* Regulations on Urban Housing Dismantling and Resettlement Administration of Chongqing
Municipality (effective on December 1 2002)
* Measures for Land Acquisition, Compensation and Resettlement of Chongqing Municipality
(Chongqing Municipal Government Decree No. 55, on September 13, 1999)
* Provisions on Compensation for Green Crops and Attachment on Acquired Land of Chongqing
Municipality (Chongqing Municipal Government decree (1995) 171)
* Administration Method of Construction Land of Chongqing Municipality (passed at No. 87 standing
meeting of Chongqing Municipal Govemment in August, 1991 and effective on September 1, 1991)
* Application and Approval Procedures for Construction Land of Chongqing Municipality (effective on
November 23, 1988)
* Fee Criteria on Urban Housing Dismantling and Resettlement of Chongqing Municipality (decided
at No. 16 Mayor meeting on April, 1995 and effective on July 1,1995)
* House Resettlement Provisions for Resettled persons from Agriculture of Chongqing Municipality
(effective July 15, 1995)
* Notice on Resettlement Fee Calculation Criteria for Resettled persons from Agriculture of
Chongqing Municipality (effective on July 15, 1995)
* Provisions on Compensation for Green Crops and Attachment on Acquired Land of Chongqing
Municipality (effective on September 15, 1995)
* Documents on compensation criteria of land requisition dismantling and resettlement, and
resettlement by involved districts and counties.

the World Bank Operational Policies: OP 4. 12 - Annex A (Involuntary Resettlement)
4.2 RELEVANT LAWS AND POLICY EXCERPTS FOR RESETTLEMENT
4.2.1 RELEVANT LAWS AND POLICY EXCERPTS FOR PERMANENTLY ACQUIRED LAND
4.2.1.1   LAW ON LAND ADMINISTRATION OF THE PEOPLE'S REPUBLIC OF CHINA
((Law on Land Administration of the People's Republic of China)) sets forth: Any unit and
individual needing land for construction has to legally apply for using state land.
Article 47: Owners whose land is acquired shall be compensated according to the original purpose
of the land before acquisition.
The compensation for acquisition of farmland shall include land compensation, resettlement
subsidy and compensation for attachments and green crops on the land. The land acquisition
compensation shall be six to ten times as much as the average annual output value of three years
before the farmland was acquired. The resettlement subsidy shall be calculated as per the number
of rural residents to be resettled. The number of rural residents to be resettled shall be calculated
by dividing the area of land acquired by the average per - capita area of land of the owning unit
before acquisition. The standard of resettlement subsidy for each rural resident to be resettled
shall be four to six times as much as the average annual output value in three years before the
farmland was acquired. However, the resettlement subsidy per hectare of acquired farmland shall
not exceed the average annual output value in three years before acquisition by 15 times at the
most.
The rate of compensation and resettlement subsidy for acquisition of other land shall be
determined by the province, autonomous region and municipality with reference to the rate of
compensation and resettlement subsidy for acquisition of farmland.
The rate of compensation for attachments and green crops on the land shall be determined by the
province, autonomous region and municipality.
In cases where the land compensation and resettlement subsidy paid under clause 2 of this article
is not enough to enable the farmers to be resettled to maintain the original living standard, the
amount of resettlement subsidy may be increased with the prior approval of the people's
government of the province, autonomous region or municipality. However, the sum total of the land
compensation and resettlement subsidy shall not be 30 times as much as the average annual
output value of the land in three years before the land was acquired.
SOGREAH CONSULTANTS- 23500321.R4 - AuGusT 2004                      PAGE 71



CHONGQING MUNICIPALITY - THE WORLD BANK
CHONGQING URBAN ENVIRONMENT PROJECT
RESETTLEMENT ACTION PLAN
4.2.1.2    RELEVANT POLICIES ON PERMANENTLY ACQUIRED LAND OF CHONGQING MUNICIPALITY
Land Administration Provisions of Chongqing Municipality
Article 19 Legal approval formalities shall be required in converting farmland to construction land.
The converted land shall comply with: (1) the land complies with overall land use planning; (2) the
land complies with the urban planning or village and township planning; (3) yearly planned data for
converted land is obtained; (4) Make - up farm land measure is implemented.
Article 22 Land compensation, resettlement subsidy, green crop and land attachment
compensation shall be completely paid within three months from the date when land compensation
and resettlement plan is approved.
Article 32 The space standard of residential house site shall be 20 to 25 m2 per person for
villagers living within the metropolitan area and 20 to 30 m2 per person for those living within non-
metropolitan districts, counties (or autonomous ethnic minority counties) and cities. Families
consisting of less than three persons shall be counted as three persons and four persons as four
and those consisting of more than five persons shall be counted as five persons. The area of land
taken in expanding the residential shall be taken into account with the space of the original house
site. The standard of land pace for building residence shall be 10 m2 per person for residences
living within the metropolitan area and 15 m2 per person for those living in non-metropolitan
districts, counties (or autonomous counties) and cities. Families consisting of less than three
persons shall be counted as three persons and four persons as four and those consisting of more
than five persons shall be counted as five persons.
Article 39 The land using unit or individual shall pay, according to the applicable laws, the land
acquisition compensation, resettlement subsidy and compensation for green crops and
attachments on the land acquired.
SOGREAH CONSULTANTS- 23500321 R4 - AUGUST 2004                      PAGE 72



CHONGQING MUNICIPALITY - THE WORLD BANK
CHONGQING URBAN ENVIRONMENT PROJECT
RESETTLEMENT ACTION PLAN
The compensation for the land acquisition shall be six to ten times as much as the average annual
output value of the farmland (multi-purpose land, pastureland, orchard land and fish - farming
water space to be regarded as farmland and two mus of other non - farming lands to be regarded
as one mu of farmland except as otherwise specified in the applicable laws or regulations, the
same rule applying hereunder) in three years before acquisition (the average annual output value
of farmland in the urban area in three years before acquisition shall be determined uniformly by the
municipal goveMment; that of individual land in the urban area shall be determined by the county -
(or city - ) standard people's government in unit of rural or urban township; and that of the
vegetable land, grain seed breeding land and special - purpose fishing pond shall be calculated as
being 1.2 to 1.5 times as much as the average annual output value of the farmland in three years
before acquisition, the same rule applying hereunder). The resettlement subsidy for the land
acquired shall be calculated according to the number of agricultural population to be resettled. The
number of agricultural population to be resettled shall be calculated by dividing the area of
farmland acquired by the area of farmland owned per capita of the unit before acquisition (the per -
capita area of farmland equals to the sum of the farmland area registered in the certificate and 0.5
times as much as the non - farming land divided by the total population of the rural collective
economic organization). The standard of resettlement subsidy for each individual of the agricultural
population shall be four to six times as much as the average annual value of the farmland in three
years before acquisition. However, the resettlement subsidy per hectare of the acquired farmland
shall not exceed 15 times as much as the average annual value of the farmland in three years
before acquisition.
In the event that the land compensation and resettlement subsidy paid as per clause 2 of this
article is not enough to enable the farmer to be resettled to maintain his original standard of living,
the amount of the resettlement subsidy may be increased with the prior approval of the municipal
people's government. However, the sum total of the land compensation and resettlement subsidy
shall not exceed 30 times as much as the average annual value of the in three years before
acquisition.
Article 41 In the case of acquiring land owned by a rural collective economic organization, the
agrarian population of that organization shall be resettled in the following way:
(1) The organization shall be disintegrated after its land is completely acquired and its members
shall have their status changed from agricultural population to non-agricultural population
(briefly referred to as status-changed hereinafter)
(2) After the land of the organization is acquired, the number of status-changed persons shall be
calculated by dividing the area of farmland acquired by the per-capita space of land before
land acquisition. The actual number of status-changed persons shall be determined jointly by
the rural or urban people's government, village committee and leadership of the affected
organization according to the area of land acquired per person or per household.
SOGREAH CONSULTANTS- 23500321 R4 - AUGUST 2004                      PAGE 73



CHONGQING MUNICIPALITY - THE WORLD BANK
CHONGQING URBAN ENVIRONMENT PROJECT
RESETTLEMENT ACTION PLAN
(3) In the event that the per-capita space of farmland is more than 0.5mu or the per-capita space
of vegetable land is more than 0.4mu after the organization's land outside the urban planning
area is partly acquired and the contracted farmland can be reallocated according to the
applicable law, the affected person may choose not to change his status by applying to the
village committee for approval. However the land user shall pay land acquisition compensation
and resettlement subsidy. The village committee shall reallocate the contracted farmland to the
affected person and assure his contractual entitlement as per the applicable law.
The involved district, county (or autonomous county) or city people's government shall resettle the
status-changed persons properly by various means such as providing monetary compensation,
land and insurance according to the actual local conditions following the principle of ensure social
stability and development. The land compensation and resettlement subsidy shall be used for the
purpose of promoting production. The specific resettlement measures shall be developed
separately by the municipal people's government.
The status-changed rural residents become urban residents and shall be managed as urban
residents.
Measures for Land Acquisition, Compensation and Resettlement of Chongqing Municipality
Article 4 Compensation for land acquired, resettlement subsidy and compensation for attachments
and green corps on the land shall be paid in accordance with Article 26 of "regulations for
Implementation of the Land Management Law of the People's republic of China"
Article 5 Compensation for acquired land, resettlement subsidy and green crops and green crops
on the land shall be paid in accordance with Article 39 of Measures for land Acquisition,
Compensation and Resettlement in Chongqing Municipality.
Article 6 The compensation for the buildings on the land shall be calculated according to the legal
area registered in the collective land tenure certificate and rural house ownership certificate. The
compensation for structures shall be calculated according to the actual area and the compensation
for green crops shall be calculated according to the actual growing area when the land is acquired.
Article 7 The compensation for ordinary trees planted in patches on the farmland without being
properly approved shall be calculated according to the compensation rate for green crops.
Trees planted in patches shall be compensated according to actual case.
Orchard, tea garden, mulberry and nursery shall be compensated according to 1.2 to 1.5 times of
the average annual output value of previous three years. For rare trees, relevant state provisions
shall apply.
Article 8 No compensation shall be made for the following buildings (structures) on the land:
House and other buildings (structures) not granted a land tenure certificate and rural house
ownership certificate;
SOGREAH CONSULTANTS - 23500321 .R4 - AUGUST 2004                   PAGE 74
s~~~~~~~~~ __         -- -- - - - - -



CHONGOING MUNICIPALITY - THE WORLD BANK
CHONGOING URBAN ENVIRONMENT PROJECT
RESETTLEMENT ACTION PLAN
Flowers, grasses, trees and crops planted and buildings (structures) erected after the date on
which the official document on land acquisition is issued by the government;
Buildings (structures) on the temporary land whose approved service period has expired or which
has no specified service period but has been used for more than two years;
Buildings (structures) built illegally on the collectively owned land;
Wild natural grasses and shrubs.
Article 13 The following personnel of the unit whose land has been acquired shall be resettled by
changing their identity from agricultural to non - agriculture resident or by changing the from of
land contracting:
Agrarian population;
Students studying at universities and polytechnic schools;
Compulsory servicemen; and
Criminals serving jail terms or personnel being re-educated through labour.
Article 14 The following personnel of the unit whose land has been acquired shall not be resettled:
Personnel whose identity been changed from agricultural to non - agricultural resident moved in
without a lawful marital relationship or fostering (supporting) relationship and who have no
contracted. land;
Retired personnel who have returned to the rural area to settle down to leave their jobs to their
children who have granted urban citizenship.
Article 15 To agriculturally resettled persons, money resettlement, insurance resettlement, land
resettlement or civil affairs department resettlement shall apply.
Article 16 For those personnel of the land to be acquired whose identity has been changed from
agricultural to non - agricultural resident who chose to be resettled in monetary form, the land
management department shall pay the land compensation and resettlement subsidy to the rural
collective economic organization to be collected by such personnel in the specific period of time or
pay them directly to such personnel.
Article 17 For male of 50 and female of 45 agriculturally resettled persons and with his or her
application, the land administration department shall pay full or half of the land compensation and
resettlement subsidy to China Life Insurance Co. Chongqing Branch as pension. The details shall
be drafted by the land department and insurance company and approved by the municipal
government.
SOGREAH CONSULTANTS - 23500321 R4 - AUGuST 2004                     PAGE 75



CHONGQING MUNICIPALITY - THE WORLD BANK
CHONGQING URBAN ENVIRONMENT PROJECT
RESETTLEMENT ACTION PLAN
Article 18 After the collective owned land is completely acquired and the enterprises, which can
accept more than 10 resettled persons, can be established, with the approval of competent
govemment, the land department can pay at one time land compensation and resettlement
subsidy to the enterprises as the contribution of the resettled persons. Meanwhile, the land of 20 -
30 m2per capita shall be allocated for developing production and resettling the resettled persons.
The enterprises shall pay land cost as legally required.
Article 19 for following persons, the land department shall pay land compensation and resettlement
subsidy to the civil affairs department at one time, and the latter shall issue subsistence fee as
stipulated or monthly:
Orphans of under 18;
Elderly males of 60 and female of 50 of no family;
Disabled persons with certificate and without guardians;
Persons with mental disease certified by the hospital above county level and without guardians.
Article 20 Land acquisition regulating fund method shall be applied to resettled person
resettlement. Regulating fund shall be 3000 Yuan per mu and collected by district (autonomous
county, town) government and 2000 by other district, county or town (autonomous county, town).
This regulating fund shall be paid by the construction land user and used for resettled person
resettlement regulation.
Relevant provisions in Forest Administration Method of Chongqing Municipality
Approved unit or individual acquiring forestland shall pay following fees:
Forestland compensation fee: Not less than 80% of the compensation criteria of cultivated land;
not less than 20% for temporarily occupied forestland for operation.
Trees and attachment compensation:
a. Young trees: Pay 300 to 500 Yuan per mu for tree planting. Pay as much as invested for heavily
invested forestland. Pay additional 300 Yuan every year for forest care (400 Yuan for economic
trees). Young trees under three years old shall be counted as three.
b. Middle aged and mature trees: Pay according to the local market price based on 6 to 10 cubic
meter per mu.
c. Protective trees: Pay as much as 3 to 5 times of the mature tree volume.
d. Nursery: Pay 10,000 to 15000 Yuan per mu.

RESETTLEMENT ACTION PLAN
e. Economic trees (including bamboo forest): Pay as much as 3 to 5 times of actual output value of
previous three years or planting and care cost.
f. Attached dismantled on the forestland shall be compensated as follows.
Resettlement subsidy: Refer to land administration code or relevant regulations.
Vegetation rehabilitation fee.
a. Pay 3 to 4 Yuan per square meter of young forestland;
b. Pay 4 to 6 Yuan per square meter of special tree land;
c. Pay 1 to 2 Yuan per square meter of other forestland.
4.2.2 RELEVANT LAW AND POLICIES ON HOUSE DISMANTLING AND RESETTLEMENT
Regulations on Urban House Dismantling and Resettlement
Article 6 Houses can be dismantled and resettled only after the permission has been obtained by
the dismantling unit.
Article 8 The dismantling person, scope and dismantling period shall be publicly announced.
Dismantling administration department and the unit shall work together to explain to the dismantled
persons.
Article 22 The dismantling person shall compensate the dismantled person as set forth herein.
Article 23 Money compensation or exchange of house property right . ...... can apply.
Article 24 Money compensation amount shall be determined according to market evaluation price.
The details shall be set forth by provincial, autonomous region and municipal governments.
Relevant Law and Policy Excerpts on House Dismantling and Resettlement of Chongqing
Municipality
Article 8 After obtaining project site permit, the construction unit shall apply with certificate to
involved house dismantling department of concerned district, county (autonomous county, town)
for suspension of handling related formalities.

The said department shall check the application without delay on receipt of the construction unit's
request, and issue notice to the land, planning, city work and industrial and commercial
administration departments of suspension of handling related formalities within seven work days if
the conditions are satisfied. If the conditions are not satisfied, non - acceptance notice in writing
shall be made in the same period.
Article 9 House dismantling and resettlement permit- must be obtained from the competent
department in dismantling houses for construction use, compensating and resettling the
dismantled persons.
Municipal house dismantling and resettlement department shall issue house dismantling and
resettlement permits to municipal key projects, construction projects involving more than one
district, county (autonomous county, town) and city proper projects requiring over 10000 m2 of
dismantled space.
Article 15 Within the resettlement period, the dismantling person and the dismantled shall sign
compensation and resettlement agreement, in which the details shall be set forth such as
compensation form, amount, resettlement house size, quality and location, transition house quality,
transition form and period and breaching.
To dismantle rented house, the dismantling person, the dismantled and renter shall sign
compensation and resettlement agreement. The signed agreement shall be submitted to the
house-dismantling department for keeping in file.
Article 16 After signing the agreement, the dismantled or renter refuses to relocate beyond the
resettlement period, the dismantling person can apply for arbitration or file a lawsuit to the people's
court. During lawsuit the dismantling person can apply to the court for advance dismantling.
Article 20 Compensation and resettlement fund shall be used only for compensation and
resettlement and not used for other purpose.
House dismantling department at municipal, district, county (autonomous county, town) levels shall
supervise the use of the compensation and resettlement fund.
Article 25 Compensation and resettlement form can be money compensation, or exchange of
house property right of same money compensation amount.
Unless otherwise legally specified, the dismantled can select compensation form.
Article 26 Money compensation amount shall be determined according to the market evaluation
price by acquiring into consideration the position, use, construction or indoor space of the house to
be dismantled.
The compensation amount of the dismantled house shall not be less than 70% of average price of
new house price of same position and same use.

Article 31 Exchange of house property right shall not apply to the attachment of dismantled public

Compensation and Resettlement Metlhod on Acquired Land of Chongqing Municipality
Article 9 Under the current method, the persons to be resettled shall be properly compensated in

Article 10 If the houses of agriculturally resettled persons are outside of the dismantling scope, no
dismantling, no compensation and no resettlement shall be made. However, based on the
residence space certified in land use certificate. One time compensation shall be paid to the
collective economic organization according to 1 to 2 times of average annual output value of
previous three years. After compensation, the resettled persons shall share equal treatment in
public facilities. If the residence space is to be acquired for state construction, house compensation
and resettlement shall be dealt with according to the land acquisition provisions.
Article 11 Water and power facilities of the acquired unit (excluding villagers of the acquired land)
shall be compensated according to the actual cost. For water conservancy facilities compensation,
refer to the relevant state regulations.
Wired broadcast and closed TV circuits, natural gas installations shall be compensated according
to actual cost. Telephone set resettlement shall be compensated according to telecommunication
department provisions. Decoration of dismantled house shall be dismounted by the owner and
shall not be compensated. The decoration, which cannot be dismounted, shall be properly
compensated.
Farmer's house modified for other purpose shall be compensated according to residential house.
Article 12 To dismantle enterprise buildings (structures) with land use certificate and other legal
certificate, after the compensation is calculated based replacement value original buildings
(structures) shall belong to the state and handled by the land department. Resettlement loss fee
(including resettlement loss, stoppage, etc.) of enterprise shall be shall be calculated according to
15% to 20% of the net value of the depreciated equipment.

built house persons, one time 300-500 Yuan per capita is issued.
4.3 WORLD BANK OPERATIONAL POLICIES ON INVOLUNTARY RESETTLEMENT
Objective of World Bank Operational Policies on Involuntary Resettlement:
* Explore all feasible project design option to avoid or reduce involuntary resettlement.
* If unavoidable, resettlement activities shall be conceived and implemented based on
sustainable.development option. Provide adequate fund to enable the resettled share the
benefit, participate the planning implementation through discussions.
*   Assist the resettled to improve livelihood, restore original living standard or higher.
To solve livelihood difficulty in compulsory resettlement, the World Bank requires the
borrower to prepare a resettlement plan or policy framework on resettlement covering.
(1) Resettlement plan or policies measures to enable the resettled persons
a. Know optional right and other right on resettlement.
b. Be aware of feasibility scheme, technically and economically, and participate in discussion and
enjoy opportunity of selection;
c. Obtain quick and effective compensation with full replacement cost so as to counteract the direct
property loss caused by the project.
SOGREAH CONSULTANTS - 23500321.R4 - AUGUST 2004                     PAGE 82



CHONGOING MUNICIPALITY - THE WORLD BANK
CHONGQING URBAN ENVIRONMENT PROJECT
RESETTLEMENT ACTION PLAN
(2) If effect involves the resettlement, then corresponding measures shall be acquired to implement
plan of the resettled resettlement or framework of the resettled resettlement policies, thus to
ensure that the resettled are able to:
a. Get help (for instance obtaining subsidy for resettlement) during the resettlement;
b. Obtain residence or homestead, or have site of agricultural production upon request. The
potential of such agricultural production site, location advantage and other comprehensive factors
shall be at least equivalent to the advantageous condition of the original site.
(3) To realize the objective of this policy, corresponding measures, as necessary, shall be acquired
to implement plan of the resettled resettlement or framework of the resettled resettlement policies,
thus to ensure that the resettled are able to:
a. Reasonably estimate the time required for resuming livelihood and living standard and a proper
transition period during which assistance is available;
b. Obtain assistance of development, such as land management, credit, training or job finding.
4.4 RESETTLEMENT POLICY OF THE PROJECT
Resettlement Policy implemented in this project is constituted based on the relevant laws of the
People's Republic of China, Chongqing Municipal Government, urban districts, counties and
(county-level) cities as well as resettlement policy of World Bank.
4.4.1 RESETTLEMENT PRINCIPLES
1)  After land acquisition and resettlement, level of production and living standard of the
resettled shall be recovered or enhanced to a relatively higher level than that before
resettlement or prior to implementation of the project.
2)  All the involuntary resettlement shall be executed as integral part of the project construction
so as to provide sufficient fund to the resettled that benefit them from the project.
SOGREAH CONSULTANTS - 23500321 R4 - AUGusT 2004                      PAGE 83



CHONGOING MUNICIPALITY - THE WORLD BANK
CHONGQING URBAN ENVIRONMENT PROJECT
RESETTLEMENT ACTION PLAN
3)  Make compensation for the property of person affected by the project. When the acquisition
of the rural collective land is carried out, all the losses shall be reasonably compensated
based on the relevant laws. The resident (farmers) affected by resettlement will obtain
resettlement house at least equivalent to the original residence in terms of traffic
convenience, various necessary installations and surrounding environment, or get
compensation equivalent to the value of their original residence. For the affected enterprises
& institutions and stores, the original business environment shall be restored as early as
possible, or let them obtain compensation equivalent to price of their houses. At the same
time, the loss of suspending business due to the project shall be also compensated. The
infrastructure shall be recovered completely so that its function is at least not lower than the
original level to maintain normal life of the nearby persons who are not resettled, within the
range of project construction. For the resettled temporarily affected by the project and those
have partial property losses and no resettlement is needed, equivalent compensation is also
possible.
4)  Labour force of the resettled shall be resettled following the principle of "making resettlement
at local place and creating multiple channels of employment". During the process, local
government, the project undertaker and village administration committee evaluated price
jointly make arrangement for employment, thereby exerting no influence on the living
standard of the resettled. Office of the project undertaker evaluated price implement a policy
of exploitation type resettlement, in which, all the forces of the local governments evaluated
price be brought into full play in training of the resettled employment and creating more job
opportunities for them. This evaluated price allow the resettled to adapt to the environment
of the resettlement points in a short time period, so that they evaluated price live through
self-reliance economically, hence the responsibility of settling the resettled evaluated price
be transferred in time from resettlement organization to the resettled themselves.
5)  Office of project evaluated price show solicitude to the resettled for their difficulties during
the resettlement and a time period after resettlement, and help them fit into community of
the resettled places as quickly as possible.
6)  The project undertaker evaluated price pays much attention to the weak group people.
During the resettlement, they are able to enjoy preferential policies such as residence and
employment. After resettlement, periodical visit shall also be paid to them, and those who
have special difficulties evaluated price receive assistance until their being transferred to
local civil administration organ.
7)  During the implementation of compiling plan of resettlement, the resettled are encouraged
participating in the process; full respect shall be given to the resettled in relation to the mode
of their resettlement.
8)  Before the construction and land taking, the resettled evaluated price obtains all expenses
they lost.
SOGREAH CONSULTANTS - 23500321 .R4 - AUSUST 2004                       PAGE 84



CHONGQING MUNICIPALITY - THE WORLD BANK
CHONGOING URBAN ENVIRONMENT PROJECT
RESETTLEMENT ACTION PLAN
9)  The project undertaker evaluated price and try its best to have maximum cost-benefit
effectiveness. The resettled resettlement organization evaluated price make great efforts to
enhance its work capability of conducting the resettled resettlement, standardize the work
behaviour of resettling the resettled, establish and perfect the interior control mechanism,
prevent waste of fund, withholding state fund, seeking private benefits and corruption so as
to make full use of the funds for resettlement and realize best effect of resettlement. In other
word, in the set index of the resettlement effectiveness, they evaluated price try all means to
reduce cost of resettlement.
4.4.2 RESETTLEMENT POLICY OF THE PROJECT
4.4.2.1   POLICY  OF COMPENSATION  FOR  LAND   ACQUISITION  AND  LABOR  FORCE
RESETTLEMENT
Policy of Compensation for Land Acquisition
1) In the case of acquiring farmland, compensation evaluated price be made depending on the
original purpose for which the land is used. The compensation includes the compensation
for land, resettlement, ground attachments and crops. The compensation for ground
attachments and crops belongs to their owner.
2) The payment of land compensation and resettlement subsidy should be made according to
the actual conditions of each district, county or city. In Tongliang County, Changshou
District, Bishan County, Wulong County, Jiangjin District and Beibei District, the land
compensation and resettlement subsidy evaluated price be paid fully to the affected rural
households. In Dazu County, the land-evaluated price is reallocated and the land
compensation and resettlement subsidy evaluated price be divided equally among the
villagers.
3) The land compensation and resettlement subsidy evaluated price be calculated according to
the number of agrarian population to be resettled, which is calculated by dividing the space
of farmland acquired by the per-capita space of farmland before land acquisition.
4) In the case of acquiring farmland, land and resettlement compensation to be paid at the rate
of 10 to 30 times as much as the average annual yield of the farmland in the past three
years.
5) In the case of acquiring garden land, the land and resettlement compensation to be paid at
the rate of 1.2 times as much as the compensation rate for farmland.
6) In the case of acquiring fish pond, the land and resettlement compensation to be paid at the
rate of 1.3 times as much as the compensation rate for farmland.
SOGREAH CONSULTANTS - 23500321 .R4 - AUGUST 2004                   PAGE 85



CHONGOING MUNICIPALITY - THE WORLD BANK
CHONGQING URBAN ENVIRONMENT PROJECT
RESETTLEMENT ACTION PLAN
7) In the case of acquiring forestland, the compensation for land, resettlement and forest is to
be paid to the owner.
8) In the case of acquiring non-farmland (such as wasteland, collective owned riverside
shallow land, etc.), the land compensation and resettlement subsidy are to be paid at the
rate of 1/2 of the rate of compensation for farmland.
9) In the case of acquiring state-owned riverside shallow land, compensation is made for the
crops on it only.
10)If the land compensation and resettlement subsidy paid as specified above cannot enable
the farmers to be resettled to live at the level before land acquisition, the amount of
resettlement subsidy may be increased as approved by the provincial people's government.
However the total amount of land compensation and resettlement subsidy should not
exceed 30 times as much as the annual yield of the land acquired.
11)1n the case of acquiring state-owned land that needs to be compensated for, compensation
evaluated price be made by the project owner in consultation with the local government,
land administration bureau and affected persons.
12)ln the case of acquiring the land owned by enterprises and institutions, compensation
evaluated price be made at the evaluated price.
13)ln the case of temporary land occupation, if the impact has not yet affected one growing
season, compensation for loss of crops evaluated price be made as if one growing season
were affected; if the impact has affected one year of growing, compensation for loss of
crops evaluated price be made as if two and half growing seasons were affected; if the
impact has affected half a year of growing, compensation evaluated price be made as if
yield of the land in one year were lost. The compensation evaluated price be paid directly to
the farmers affected by land acquisition and should not be lower than the loss caused to the
farmers. For the rehabilitation of land temporarily taken, the constructor evaluated price re-
cultivate the farmland acquired after construction is completed and return it to the village
and the village committee evaluated price accept the re-cultivated land in collaboration with
the related agencies.
Policy of Labour Resettlement
All the affected labour forces shall be properly resettled.
The affected villagers shall be resettled in three ways: status-changing, monetary compensation
and land reallocation, and the status-changed persons affected by land acquisition may be
resettled by providing monetary compensation, insurance, endowment insurance and minimum
subsistence allowance.

Other Policies
1) The compensation fees for land and sum of compensation for resettlement evaluated price be
exempted from any tax & fees and relevant court costs.
2) The resettlement executor evaluated price help the resettled in making change of registered
permanent residence and transferring schooling of their children.
4.4.2.2   POLICIES FOR URBAN RESIDENT RESETTLEMENT
First, based on the replacement value, the demolished houses shall be evaluated by an Evaluation
Organization with Qualification of evaluating urban houses according to the factors such as
location, use and building area or service area. The evaluation organization shall be chosen by the
people whose houses are demolished. The evaluating organization, before fixing the evaluation
price of the real estate market of the demolished houses, shall listen to the opinion of the persons
whose houses are demolished. The actual compensation should be adjusted based on the
evaluated price at the time of demolishment.
Policy of Resettlement
The resettled person may, after receiving the house compensation (inducing land price), choose to
get resettled in different ways according to theirfinancial capabilities and personal preference such
as purchasing uniformly constructed resettlement houses, commercial houses or second-hand
houses, and renting cheap-rent houses provided by the local government.
Subsidy Policy During Resettlement
*   For the resettled families equipped with telephone sets, cable TV and other devices,
compensation for relocating such facilities shall be made at the prevailing standard of charge
set by the companies to which these facilities belong.
* The demolisher shall pay the movement allowance and transition allowance to the actual user
of the residential house.
*   Each resettled household shall receive a bounty for moving out of their house within the
specified time limit.
Other Policies
*   During the resettlement period, the resettled persons shall be exempted from any relevant tax
and fees.
*   Person in charge of resettlement shall help the resettled in making change of registered
permanent residence and transferring schooling of their children.
SOGREAH CONSULTANTS - 23500321 R4 - AUGUST 2004                    PAGE 87



CHONGOING MUNICIPALITY - THE WORLD BANK
CHONGQING URBAN ENVIRONMENT PROJECT
RESETTLEMENT ACTION PLAN
*   Offer assistance to the weak group people, and for details, refer to 4.4.2.5 Policies of
Resettlement.
*   No illegal building and temporary building beyond expiry period are found in actual
investigation of the project. If such a case is found during actual resettlement, compensation
shall be made in accordance with replacement price of the building.
4.4.2.3   POLICIES FOR RESETTLING RURAL RESETTLED RESIDENT
Policies of Compensation
Compensation for demolition rural residential houses shall be made according to the replacement
principle.
Policy of Resettlement
The resettled persons may, after receiving the house compensation, choose to get resettled in
different ways according to their financial capabilities and personal preference. These
arrangements include building houses themselves, purchasing uniformly built cheap resettlement
houses commercial houses or second-hand houses or renting low-rent houses provided by the
government. In the former case, the resettlement agency shall pay compensation to the owner of
the house demolished and at the same time provide him free of charge with a house site at the
space standard of 30m2 per person (families consisting of less than 3 persons to be counted as 3
persons, 4 persons as 4 and more than 5 persons as 5). In the latter two cases, the resettlement
agency shall pay the affected household compensation not only for the house demolished but also
the house site taken.
Subsidy Policy During the Resettlement
(1) For the resettled families equipped with telephone sets, cable TV and other devices,
compensation for relocating such facilities shall be made at the prevailing standard of charge
set by the companies to which these facilities belong.
(2) The demolisher shall pay the movement allowance and transition allowance to the actual user
of the residential house.
(3) Each resettled household shall receive a bounty for moving out of their house within the
specified time limit.
Other Policies
(1) During the resettlement period, the resettled will be exempted from any relevant tax and fees.
SOGREAH CONSULTANTS- 23500321 .R4 - AUGUST 2004                     PAGE 88



CHONGQING MUNICIPALITY - THE WORLD BANK
CHONGOING URBAN ENVIRONMENT PROJECT
RESETTLEMENT ACTION PLAN
(2) Person in charge of resettlement shall help the resettled in making change of registered
permanent residence and transferring schooling of their children.
(3) Offer assistance to the weak group people, and for details, refer to 4.4.2.5 Policies of
Resettlement.
(4) No illegal building and temporary buildings beyond expiry period are found in actual
investigation of the project. If such a case is found during actual resettlement, compensation
shall be made in accordance with replacement price of the building.
4.4.2.4   POLICIES OF RESETTLEMENT FOR AFFECTED ENTERPRISES & INSTITUTIONS AND
SHOPS
Policies of Compensation
Evaluation shall first be made of the houses and land of the affected enterprises, institutions and
shops. The owners of such enterprises, institutions and shops shall be compensated not only for
the loss of land, houses and attachments thereto but also for the financial losses incurred to them.
The entitlements and interests including salaries, medical care, social security, dividend, bonus,
etc. of their employees shall not be affected during relocation, and no employee shall lose his/her
job due to relocation of the enterprise, institute or shop for which he/she works.
Other Policies
(1) During the period of resettlement and recovery, the affected enterprises & institutions and
stores are exempted from any relevant tax & fees.
(2) No building involving violation of rules and temporary buildings beyond expiry period are found
in actual investigation of the project. If such a case is found during actual resettlement,
compensation shall be made in accordance with replacement price of the building.
4.4.2.5    POLICIES FOR RESETTLEMENT OF VULNERABLE GROUP
Except the policies described above, the vulnerable groups shall enjoy the following preferential
policies.

CHONGQING MUNICIPALITY - THE WORLD BANK
CHONGQING URBAN ENVIRONMENT PROJECT
RESETTLEMENT ACTION PLAN
(1) According to their desire, the land compensation fees and sum of compensation may either be
given to Civil Administration Bureau of County or county (village) rest home or their children,
then the Administration Bureau or rest home or their children will be responsible for looking
after them in their old age.
(2) For the vulnerable group people affected by the demolished house, those who are difficult in
residence, some mode of assistance shall be provided to them, for instance the supply of
cheap-rent house. At the same time, training will be delivered to labour force in the family of
such vulnerable group people. Information on various opportunities for job and guidance in this
regard will be provided to them, thus enabling them to have more opportunities for finding a
job.
(3) For the vulnerable group people who will build house themselves, the resettlement executor
shall help them during the house building. Meanwhile, training of agricultural technique will
delivered to their children free of charge so as to help them in developing agricultural
production to increase income from agriculture.
(4) For the family of such vulnerable group people affected by temporary land acquisition, priority
shall be given to them for restoring their land.
(5) During the project construction, priority shall be given to children of such vulnerable group
family in recruiting them to do some job with low technical requirement.
4.4.2.6    POLICIES OF COMPENSATION FOR AFFECTED INFRASTRUCTURE AND LAND ATTACHMENT
For the affected infrastructures and land attachments, the demolisher shall give compensation to
the owner of title at the rate of replacement cost, who will resume the rebuilding of such
infrastructures and land attachments.

5 COMPENSATION RATES
The following rates of compensation for damages caused by this project are formulated according
to the legal framework presented in the preceding section and in consideration of the actual
situation of the counties and districts involved.
5.1 DEMOLITION AND RESETTLEMENT OF URBAN RESIDENTS' HOUSES
See
TABLE 5-1 for rates of compensation for demolition of houses of different structure types, which
are based on the displacement prices including the land price surveying and calculating in
March 2004 by RAP preparation team.
5.2 DEMOLITION AND RESETTLEMENT OFRURAL RESIDENTS' HOUSES
See
TABLE 5-2 for rates of compensation. for demolition of houses of different structure types, which
are based on the displacement prices surveying and calculating in March 2004 by RAP preparation
team.
5.3 RATES OF COMPENSATION FOR ENTERPRISES
The compensation for resettlement of enterprises includes the compensation for houses, financial
subsidy (in compensation for losses due to discontinuation of operation), compensation for
facilities and subsidy for movement. See TABLE 5-3 for detailed compensation rates, which are
based on evaluation of the land and demolished houses of the affected enterprises.
5.4 RATES OF COMPENSATION FOR INSTITUTIONS
The compensation for resettlement of institutions includes the compensation for houses, financial
subsidy, compensation for facilities and subsidy for movement. See TABLE 5-4 for detailed
compensation rates which are based on evaluation of the land and demolished houses of the
affected institutions.
5.5 RATES OF COMPENSATION FOR AFFECTED SHOPS
The compensation for the affected shops includes the compensation for houses, financial subsidy,
compensation for resettlement of facilities and subsidy for movement. See TABLE 5-5 for detailed
compensation rates, which are based on evaluation of the land and demolished houses of the
affected shops.
SOGREAH CONSULTANTS - 23500321 .R4 - AuGUST 2004                    PAGE 91



CHONGOING MUNICIPALITY - THE WORLD BANK
CHONGQING URBAN ENVIRONMENT PROJECT
RESETTLEMENT ACTION PLAN
5.6 COMPENSATION FOR ACQUISITION OF COLLECTIVE-OWNED LAND
In line with the stipulations of the "PRC Land Management Law", 'Chongqing Municipal
Regulations regarding Land Management", "Chongqing Municipal Measures for Compensation for
Land Acquisition" and applicable local policies and regulations of the counties and districts
involved, the compensation for land acquisition includes the compensation for land, subsidy for
resettlement and compensation for crops. See TABLE 5-6 and
TABLE 5-7 for detail.
5.7 COMPENSATION FOR TEMPORARY LAND OCCUPATION
According to the regulations concerning the temporary land occupation promulgated by Chongqing
municipal government and county and district governments involved, crop compensation shall be made for
the temporary land occupation . In principle, compensation for loss of crops shall be calculated in that a way
that an affected period of shorter one quarter shall be regarded as one quarter and one year as 2.5 quarters
or half a year as one year. The constructor shall restore the land to its original condition. See TABLE 5-8 for
the rates of compensation for temporary use of land.
5.8 COMPENSTION RATES FOR INFRASTRUCTURES AND GROUND ATTACHMENTS
TABLE 5-9 contains the rates of compensation for various types of infrastructures and ground
attachments.

RESETTLEMENT ACTION PLAN
6   PRODUCTION AND LIVELIHOOD REHABILITATION PLAN
6.1 RESETTLEMENT PLAN
6.1.1 REHABILITATION OF PERMANENTLY LAND ACQUISITION
Farmers whose land is permanently acquired shall be reasonably compensated at the rate of
RMB21,450-45,000/mu. The affected persons may choose from the following three alternatives for
production resettlement:
1) Reallocation of farmland, by which the farmland is reallocated among the villages and the
land compensation and resettlement subsidy received after reallocation are divided
equally among villagers. Dazu County will adopt the method.
2) Monetary compensation: by which farmers in villages where the per-capita space of
farmland after land acquisition is more than 0.5 mu are resettled by monetary
compensation, that is, the land compensation and resettlement subsidy are paid to the
affected persons depending on the space of land taken.
3) Change of status by which farmers in villages where the per-capita space of farmland is
less than 0.5mu are resettled by having their status as agricultural population changed into
non-agricultural population. These people will thus receive a sum of RMB1.6 as land
compensation and resettlement subsidy After the number of status-changed persons is
decided, the farmland given up by them may be reallocated among villagers remaining in
the village depending on their willingness.
The status-changed farmers affected by land acquisition. may be resettled by monetary
compensation, insurance, social security support, etc.
1) Monetary compensation, by which the land compensation and resettlement subsidy are
paid to the status-changed persons to allow them to make a living;
2) Resettlement by basic social endowment insurance, by which those who are above 16
years of age but have not yet reached the age of retirement specified by the state
government may, by presenting their urban resident register and ID card, apply for the
basic endowment insurance for urban workers at the local social insurance agency. Those
who have secured this type of insurance and have actually paid the premium for 15 years
and longer may receive endowment insurance money on a monthly basis after they have
reached the age of 60 years for men and 55 years for women.
3) Resettlement by social security support, by which those status-changed persons may
apply for the minimum urban resident subsistence allowance if the average income of
them and their family members living together is lower than the minimum local subsistence
level of urban residents. The level of the allowance is determined according to the cost of
clothing, food and shelter necessary to maintain a decent life for a local urban resident
and in consideration of the cost of water and fuel (coal or gas) and compulsory schooling
of their young children. The standard of urban minimum subsistence allowance in the
affected  localities  are  respectively:  RMB185/person/month  in  Beibei  District,
RMB145/month in Jiangjin County, Changshou District, Tongliang County and Bishan
County, RMB115/person/month in Wulong County and RMB130/personlmonth in Dazu
County.
SOGREAH CONSULTANTS- 23500321.R4 - AUGUS 2004                       PAGE 101



CHONGQING MUNICIPALITY - THE WORLD BANK
CHONGQING URBAN ENVIRONMENT PROJECT
RESETTLEMENT ACTION PLAN
For those farmers losing farmland, the local government will establish a complete labor service
system to provide assistance to them. The relevant labor service agency for the affected people will
be founded one month before land acquisition to help the resettled person get employed through all
possible channels. Such help includes, for example, giving the status-changed persons free access
to the job market, collecting job information from the local sources and providing it to the displace
persons one month before land acquisition and then publishing such information once a month
afterwards, providing free vocational training to the status-changed persons (such training is mainly
oriented to the demand of the local job market. For instance, in Dazu County, the training is
oriented to the acquisition of metalworking skills, and in Bishan County, it is oriented to the
acquisition of shoe-making skills, etc.). The labor service agency will also consult the enterprises
being constructed or seeking expansion and provide them with certain preferential incentive
policies (such as being exempted from part of tax if they employ the status-changed persons) in
order to make it easier for these persons to get employed.
6.1.2 HOUSE-REBUILDING PLAN
The house-rebuilding plan involves 66 urban households, 122 rural households, 18 enterprises and
institutions, and 38 shops.
(1) Rehabilitation of urban and rural residential houses
These projects will cause the demolition and relocation of 11,288,9m2 of urban residences,
affecting 330 persons in 66 households and 16,283.1m2 of rural residences, affecting 420 persons
in 122 households. After receiving the compensation at the replacement price, the affected persons
may choose to purchase cheap uniformly constructed resettlement apartments, new commercial
apartments or second-hand apartments. In addition, the rural residents may choose to build their
own houses.
Those who purchase cheap resettlement houses may buy such houses at the compensation price and
at the space standard of 18 m2 (17m2 in Tongliang County) per person. For limitation of design, the excessive
space is to be purchased at a rate 50% as much as the construction cost if it is not more than 5m2 and if the
space is in excess of 5m2 but less than the space of the demolished house, it may be purchased at the
combination price (construction cost plus land price). Any part exceeding the space of the demolished house is
to be purchased at the market price of a commercial house. The demolisher shall construct facilities such as
water and ground leveling in the resettlement area; water and power supplies shall be constructed
as planned. Those who choose monetary compensation and purchase commercial houses in the
affected localities may be exempted from the tax derived from the 1 8m2 (1 7m2 in Tongliang County)
per person space standard. For those who cannot afford to buy commercial apartments,
resettlement houses or second-hand houses, the local government shall provide cheap rent
houses after they have received the compensation.
Rural residents who choose to build their own houses by themselves shall be provided with sites
free of charge by the local government at the average per-capita space standard. They shall build
such houses according to the plan made by the village or township.
Facilities such as water; power and gas supplies, transportation, communications and cable TV
systems shall be constructed in the resettlement areas and commercial residential centers.
Schools, post offices, banks, food markets, bus stops, hospitals and other facilities shall be
constructed around the residential area to convenience the residents. The resettled persons may
choose to buy apartments of different grades in the residential area at their own will. These houses
are much better than their former houses (most of which were built in the 1970s to 1 980s) in quality,
structure, environment and accessibility. The second-hand houses are mostly old houses left by
the enterprises and institutions and are also better than their former houses in location, quality and
structure. Part of the vulnerable group suffering domestic poverty shall be provided with cheap-rent
houses by the government.
SOGREAH CONSULTANTS - 23500321 R4 - AUGUST 2004                      PAGE 102



CHONGQING MUNICIPALITY - THE WORLD BANK
CHONGQING URBAN ENVIRONMENT PROJECT
RESETTLEMENT ACTION PLAN
(2) Affected enterprises
These projects will affect 15 enterprises, of which two are no longer in production, one operates
seasonally and one is not running well. Three enterprises are affected by land acquisition only, six
are to be completely relocated and the rest are to be partly demolished. Enterprises whose land is
acquired will receive land compensation at the estimated land price, while those to be completely
relocated may, after receiving the compensation for construction land and buildings, choose to
move into the local industrial parks or planned new urban areas. As the transportation,
supplementary facilities and environment are uniformly planned; such enterprises will have better
operating conditions than before. The income loss of the employees of such enterprises during the
transition period will be compensated for. Enterprises to be partly demolished may choose to
rebuild their houses or use the compensation for other purposes.
(3) Affected institutions
The proposed projects will affect three institutions including two whose old offices are to be
demolished. These two institutions have new offices and will receive house compensation. The
Shuren College partly demolished will rebuild backwards.
(4) Affected shops
The projects will affect 38 shops of which 36 are to be completely demolished and relocated and 34
of them are located in Dazu County. These shops are all on the ground floor of the building of
which the second floor serves as the domestic living area. Two shops in Wulong County will not be
demolished and only their operation will be temporarily affected during construction of the project.
The 36 affected shops are all run by the families and these families will receive compensation at
the displacement price with which they can purchase shops of a similar floor space and structure in
similar locations. The shop owners may choose to purchase shops to continue operation or use the
compensation for other investments.
The two affected shops in Wulong County are operated on rent. The tenants can. be resettled in
two ways: in the first place, the demolisher provides the tenants houses that can be rented as
shops including shops of similar location and rent rate and helps them look for and arrange new
production houses. The tenants shall receive a movement allowance at the rate of RMB15/m2. The
owners of both shops shall receive compensation for loss of rent. In the second place, the
pennants shall be compensated for loss of income (including wages) due to discontinuation of
operation during the period of temporary impact and the owners of the two shops shall be paid a
compensation for loss of rent at the rate of RMB20,000 per year, which can be calculated
according to the actual duration of impact.
6.2 PROJECT IN TONGLIANG COUNTY
The project will acquire 221.32 mu of land for permanent use and 37.8 mu of land for temporary
use, affecting 57 people in 13 rural households, 26 people in 5 urban households, 41 people in 2
enterprises or institutions, 4 people in 2 shops. Altogether 2,898.71m2 of houses will be
demolished, affecting 819 people in 194 households, and 308 people need to be resettled by
production.

6.2.1 REHABILITATION OF PERMANENT LAND ACQUISITION
6.2;1.1    ANALYSIS OF IMPACT CAUSED BY LAND ACQUISITION
The project will permanently acquire 221.31 mu of land, which includes 161.33 mu of farmland,
3.35 mu of garden, 54.45 mu of forest, and 2.18 mu of fish pond, affecting 693 people in 4 villages
of Bachuan Township, and 308 people need to be resettled by production.
The sewage treatment plant project will acquire 64.95 mu of land, including 57.3 mu of farmland,
3.15 mu of garden, and 4.5 mu of forest. The flood-preventing embankment work will acquire
156.36 mu of land, including 104.03 mu of farmland,.0.2 mu of garden, 49.95 mu of forest and 2.18
mu of fishpond.
See TABLE 6-1 for the impact on the affected villages.

Table 6-1 shows that Yantu receives the greatest impact of the project. Currently there are 987
people and 323 mu of farmland in Yandu Village. The project will acquire 42.02 mu of farmland,
affecting 248 people in 62 rural households, and 127 need to be resettlement by production. The
land acquired accounts for 13% of the total area of farmland. Before acquisition, the per-capita
space of farmland is 0.33 mu and after acquisition, it becomes 0.28 mu, down by 7%. If the
average annual turnover of one mu of farmland is RMB1, 258, the per-capita annual income will
reduce by RMB63. As the per-capita income of this village was RMB2, 964 in 2003, land
acquisition will reduce it by about 2%. The contribution of agriculture and secondary and tertiary
industries to the income is respectively 8% and 92% (with the secondary and tertiary industries
calculated as a whole).
Obviously, the major source of income of the labourers affected by the project is from the
secondary and tertiary industries and land acquisition will cause no significant impact on their
income.

6.2.1.2   REHABILITATION OF INCOME
(1) Resettlement plan
Through repeated consultation with the affected villagers, the following resettlement alternatives
will be provided for this project:
(D Changing status
Affected by land acquisition in construction of the project, the per-capita space of farmland of the
residents in Yandu Village will be not yet 0.3 mu and that in Tiyu Village not yet 0.5mu. Therefore
the affected labourers in both villages may choose to be resettled by having their status changed.
Each status-changed person may receive land compensation, resettlement subsidy and crop
compensation totalling RMB17,000. As the four villagers are all located in the planned expansion
area of the county seat, their land will be gradually taken in the next few years in the ongoing
urbanization process, the affected labourers in other two villages may choose to get resettled by
having their status changed. If some villagers who can have their status changed but are not willing
to do so, the village committee will resettle them by reallocating farmland among the villagers, that
is, the land given up by those who are not affected by land acquisition but are willing to have their
status changed will be reallocated to the former and the latter will have their status changed and
receive land compensation and resettlement subsidy.
(2) Monetary compensation
Those affected farmers who are willing to remain in the rural area to contact land for farming rather
than having their status changed will receive land compensation and resettlement subsidy
depending on the space of land taken from the resettlement agency at the rate of RMB30,000 per
mu.
Based on the current deposit interest rate of 2.79% for 5 years term, excluding tax on interest rate
20%, the real deposit rate is 2.232%. If the affected deposit the compensation RMB30, 000 in the
bank for 50 years, they will get about RMB997 each year, which is more than their current yearly
net income RMB1 50 from cultivated land.
) Livelihood support
The status-changed persons may enjoy the basic endowment insurance and minimum subsistence
allowance for urban residents. Those who have secured basic endowment insurance and have
actually paid the premium for 15 years and longer may receive endowment insurance money on a
monthly basis after they have reached the age of 60 years (for men) and 55 years (for women). In
Tongliang County, the minimum subsistence allowance is paid RMB145/month, which is RMB482
more than their average annual income of RMB1,258 from farming.
For those villagers who have chosen to get resettled by receiving monetary compensation and
whose families include surplus labourers, the village committee will provide them with training on
agricultural production technology and help them restructure their farming business to improve
income, such as developing greenhouse vegetable planting using the advantage of being close to
the urban area.
The local government will establish a complete labour service system to provide assistance to the
affected villagers such as providing them with information on employment, vocational training,
consultation with the local enterprises, etc. to pave the way for them to get employed.

opportunities for the rural labour force (See TABLE 6-2). The local government will help the
affected labourers to get employment through training, providing employment information and
discussions with the enterprises. In this way, they can get a monthly wage of RMB400-800 and
their income level will restore or get even higher than it used to be.

6.2.2 REHABILITATION OF TEMPORARY LAND OCCUPATION
The temporary occupation of land for this project involves five villages of Bachuan Township.
Altogether 37.8 mu of land will be occupied including 21.6 mu of collective-owned land. Crop
compensation for land temporarily occupied will be paid in such as manner that the loss in one year
of occupation will be compensated for as 2.5 quarters, which means a total sum of compensation
money of RMB2,500. Constructing the project will occupy the land for about one year and the
compensation obtained is much higher than the actual loss as the average annual output value of
the farmland is only RMB1, 200 per mu. Therefore, the farmers' livelihood will not be affected.
After the project is completed, the affected choose how to restore the land. The constructor re-
cultivates the farmland occupied and retums it to the affected; village and group organize to check
and accept.
6.2.3 REHABILITATION OF URBAN RESIDENTIAL HOUSES
The resettlement of urban residents' houses for constructing this project in Bachuan Township will
involve 26 people in 5 households, totaling563.79m2. Residents whose houses have been
demolished will be resettled by monetary compensation (the standard being RMB400 per m2 for
brick+concrete structure houses and RMB350 per m2 for brick+wood structure houses, land prices
included). The affected people receiving the compensation money have three alternatives to make,
namely, to buy houses at a preferential price, purchase commercial houses and rent cheap-rent
houses.
SOGREAH CONSULTANTS - 23500321 .R4 - AUGUST 2004                      PAGE 106



CHONGOING MUNICIPALITY - THE WORLD BANK
CHONGOING URBAN ENVIRONMENT PROJECT
RESETTLEMENT ACTION PLAN
(1) The resettled persons may choose to buy resettlement houses provided by the government at
a reduced price. They may buy such houses at the price equivalent to the compensation and at
the space standard of 17m2 per person. For limitation of design, the excessive space is to be
purchased at a rate 50% as much as the combination price (construction cost and land price
included), if it is not more than 5m2 and if the space is in excess of 5m2 but less than the space
of the former house demolished, it is may be purchased at the combination price. Any part
exceeding the space of the former house demolished is to be purchased at the price of
commercial houses. The demolisher is responsible for smoothing the ground and providing
water, power and gas supplies to the affected households.
The resettlement area is located in the planned new urban area and complete with various
supplementary facilities and well-developed transportation and communication. There is a road
system based on the G319 national highway route and the highway connectivity has reached a
total distance of 2,516 km. There, the 'five industries and one zone" (namely, the strontium salt
industry, building material industry, metallurgical and mechanical machining industry, silk and
garment industry, farm product processing industry and West Chongqing Technology Park)
have acquired shape. Furthermore, the newly built houses are much better than the former
houses in structure and quality and the resettled persons will feel more convenient than before
in livelihood, work and their children's schooling. They will notice dramatic improvement in
living standard and quality.
(2) For families who are not willing to purchase houses provided at a preferential price or built their
own houses on sites provided free, they might use the compensation money received to
purchase commercial houses in the city. The compensation should include the iand price,
which enables them to buy new or second-hand houses in Tongliang County. There is a rich
supply of new and second-hand houses in Tongliang County. The new house buildings are
fully equipped and built at places with convenient transportation facilities. The second-hand
house buildings are houses left by many enterprises and institutions. They are relatively
convenient in location and good in structure In comparison with the resettled person's former
houses (which were mostly built in the 1980s and are inferior in quality and structure), these
houses, whether they are uniformly constructed by the government or self-build by the resettled
persons or are new commercial houses or second-hand houses, are much better in quality,
structure and location. What is more, those who purchase commercial houses in Tongliang
County will be exempted from all the purchase fees and taxes. See TABLE 6-3 for information
about the supply of new commercial houses and second-hand houses.
(3) Those who cannot afford commercial houses and resettlement houses should be provided
cheap-rent houses by the government.
6.2.4 REHABILITATION OF RURAL RESIDENTIAL HOUSES
The resettlement of rural residents' houses for constructing this project in Bachuan Township will
involve 57 people in 13 households, totalling 1714.07m2 . Residents whose houses have been
demolished will be resettled by monetary compensation (the standard being RMB220 per m2 for
brick+concrete structure houses, RMB206 per m2 for brick+wood structure houses and RMB55 per
m2 for simple structure houses, land prices not included). The affected people receiving the
compensation money have three alternatives to make, namely, to construct their own houses, buy
resettlement houses at a preferential price, and purchase commercial houses. In the former case,
the resettlement agency shall pay compensation to the owner of the house demolished and at the
same time provide him free of charge with a house site. In the latter two cases, the resettlement
agency shall pay the affected household compensation not only for the house demolished but also
the house site taken.

6.2.5  RESETTLEMENT OF ENTERPRISES, INSTITUTIONS AND SHOPS
The project will affect 41 people in 2 enterprises and institutions with houses to be demolished
totalling 225.5 m2 in space, and 4 people in 2 shops with 395.35m2 of houses to be demolished.
The enterprises and institutions whose houses are to be demolished chose to get monetary
compensation and decided not to rebuild the houses. The fish-breeding centre can get
compensation for its farmland being permanently occupied and will receive a total amount of
RMB187,200 as resettlement subsidy and crop compensation. In addition, the three brick+concrete
guardhouses demolished will be compensated for at the rate of RMB220/m2 as if they were bought
new. Since the centre decided not to rebuild the houses, it can get compensation for the loss of
house site (at the rate of RMB9, 600 per mu for rural house sites). Thus the total compensation for
houses is RMB123, 100. The affected employees of the fish-breeding center are all migrant
workers and the project-executing agency will inform them 2 months before land acquisition take
place so that they have sufficient time to get reemployed.
Bachuan Township Enterprise Office has only one empty house to be demolished and therefore its
demolition will not affect the office's normal work. As the office is an institution whose land was
provided by the government free of charge, it can get the house compensation only.
Since all the shops to be demolished were made by the owners from part of their residences, they
are all willing to get resettled by getting house sites provided by the government after receiving
compensation for house demolition and loss of operation income to build their own houses. In the
resettlement area, they may chose to build multi-storry houses with the ground floor used as the
shop for business. The demolisher is responsible for smoothing the ground and providing water,
power and gas supplies to the area. As the resettlement area is located in the planned new urban
area with complete supplementary facilities and well-developed transportation and communications
systems, the affected shop owners can expect an improved business atmosphere.
See TABLE 6-4 and TABLE 6-5 for the resettlement of the affected enterprises, institutions and
shops.

demolition and one by land acquisition only. Zhou Xinghui and Zhang Jiankang are one family
living separately. Because their house to be demolished is fairly large in floor space, the
compensation enables them to self-build houses on sites provided to them free of charge. In the
process of building construction, the village committee will offer assistance.
For those vulnerable groups affected by land acquisition, the land compensation and resettlement
subsidy may be paid to their children who take the responsibility for arranging their livelihood. The
village leadership will offer vocational training for the labourers in their families or provide them with
employment information and instruction to make it easier for them to get employed.

6.3 PROJECT IN DAZU COUNTY
*The project will acquire 125.36 mu of land for permanent use and 27.6 mu of land for temporary
use, affecting 62 people in 19 rural households, 298 people in 60 urban households, 38 people in 2
enterprises and institutions, and 164 people in 34 shops. Altogether 15,449 m2 of houses will be
demolished, affecting 1,070 people in 215 households, and 337 people need to be resettled by
production.
6.3.1 REHABILITATION OF PERMANENT LAND ACQUISTION
6.3.1.1   ANALYSIS OF IMPACT CAUSED BY LAND ACQUISITION
The project will permanently acquire 125.36 mu of collective-owned land, all being dry field,
affecting 482 people in 5 villages of Longshui Township, and 337 people need to be resettled by
production.
The sewage treatment plant will acquire 56.76 mu of land and the flood-preventing embankment
works will acquire 90.6 mu of land.
